=== C:\Users\vmadmin\source\repos\Fachspezi_in_C\ShopBackend.API\Controllers\AuditLogController.cs ===
using Azure.Core;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using ShopBackend.Application.DTOs;
using ShopBackend.Application.Interfaces;
using System.Reflection;



namespace ShopBackend.API.Controllers
{
    [ApiController]

    //das [controller] wird bei der Ausgabe der URL automatisch durch den Klassennamen ersetzt, also hier praktisch api/auditLog/5 ( z.B. 5 für Id = 5 bei GetById). 
    [Route("api/[controller]")]
    [Authorize (Roles = "Admin")]
    public class AuditLogController : ControllerBase
    {
        // private readonly friert den Zugriff auf das Feld ein, es kann nur im Konstruktor gesetzt werden, danach ist es read-only.
        // Das ist best practice, um sicherzustellen, dass die Abhängigkeit nicht versehentlich geändert wird.
        private readonly IAuditLogService _auditLogService;

               /* Request kommt rein -> api/auditLog/...
                    * ASP.NET Core: "Ich brauche einen OrderController"
                    * Schaut in den Konstruktor: "Der braucht einen IAuditLogService"
                    * Holt den IAuditLogService aus dem DI-Container(der im Program.cs mit den builder.Services registriert wurde.)
                    * Erstellt den Controller mit dem Service
                    * Führt den Endpoint (die jeweilige Methode z.B. HttpGet) aus
                    * Controller wird am Ende jeweils wieder weggeworfen ->  Die Controller existieren nur einen Moment, bis deren Aufgabe/Methode erfüllt wurde.
               */
        public AuditLogController(IAuditLogService auditLogService) // <- Das ist der Konstruktor; ohne den wäre eine Dependency Injection für ASP.Net Core nicht möglich.
        {
            // das _ hier hat keine reale Auswirkung, es ist nur Konvention, um private Felder von lokalen Variablen zu unterscheiden.
            // Es könnte auch einfach auditLogService oder banana heißen, aber das _ macht es übersichtlicher.
            _auditLogService = auditLogService;
        }


        [HttpGet]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetAll()
        {
            var auditLogs = await _auditLogService.GetAllAsync();
            return Ok(auditLogs);
        }

        [HttpGet("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetById(int id)
        {
            var auditLog = await _auditLogService.GetByIdAsync(id);
            return Ok(auditLog);
        }

        [HttpGet("changedBy/{changedBy}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetByChangedBy(string changedBy)
        {
            var auditLog = await _auditLogService.GetByChangedByAsync(changedBy);
            return Ok(auditLog);
        }

        [HttpGet("entityId/{entityId}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetByEntityId(int entityId)
        {
            var auditLog = await _auditLogService.GetByEntityIdAsync(entityId);
            return Ok(auditLog);    
        }

        [HttpPost]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Create(CreateAuditLogDto dto)
        {
            var auditLog = await _auditLogService.CreateAsync(dto);
            // wieder ...(nameof(Endpoint Name), new {Routen Parameter}, Response Body)
            return CreatedAtAction(nameof(GetById), new { id = auditLog.Id }, auditLog);
        }

    }
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using ShopBackend.Application.DTOs;
using ShopBackend.Application.Interfaces;


namespace ShopBackend.API.Controllers
{
    [ApiController]
    [Route("api/[controller]")]
    
    public class CustomerController : ControllerBase
    {
        private readonly ICustomerService _customerService;
        public CustomerController(ICustomerService customerService)
        {
            _customerService = customerService;
        }


        [Authorize(Roles = "Admin")]
        [HttpGet]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetAll()
        {
            var customers = await _customerService.GetAllAsync();
            return Ok(customers);
        }

        [Authorize] // Neu: Kollission mit dem Policy Handler, Sicherheit im Service implementiert.
        [HttpGet("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetById(int id)
        {
            var customer = await _customerService.GetByIdAsync(id);
            return Ok(customer);
        }

        [Authorize(Roles = "Admin,Staff")]
        [HttpGet("findBy/{email}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetByEmail(string email)
        {
            var customer = await _customerService.GetByEmailAsync(email);
            return Ok(customer);

        }

        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")]
        [HttpPost("{userId}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Create(int userId, [FromBody] CreateCustomerDto dto)
        {
            var customer = await _customerService.CreateAsync(userId, dto);
            return CreatedAtAction(nameof(GetById), new { id = customer.Id }, customer);
        }

        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")]
        [HttpPut("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Update(int id, UpdateCustomerDto dto)
        {
            await _customerService.UpdateAsync(id, dto);
            return NoContent();
        }

        [Authorize(Roles ="Admin")]
        [HttpDelete("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Delete(int id)
        {
            await _customerService.DeleteAsync(id);
            return NoContent(); 
        }
    }
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using ShopBackend.Application.Interfaces;
using ShopBackend.Application.DTOs;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;




namespace ShopBackend.API.Controllers
{

    [ApiController]
    [Route("api/[controller]")]

    public class DiscountCodeController : ControllerBase    
    {
        private readonly IDiscountCodeService _discountCodeService;

        public DiscountCodeController(IDiscountCodeService discountCodeService)
        {
            _discountCodeService = discountCodeService;
        }

        [Authorize(Roles = "Admin")]
        [HttpGet]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetAll()
        {
            var discountCodes = await _discountCodeService.GetAllAsync();
            return Ok(discountCodes);
        }

        [Authorize] // Könnte man für user sperren, allerdings möchten die sicherlich auch gerne sehen ob Code xyz gültig ist und welche Vorrausetzungen ein Code hat. 
        [HttpGet("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetById(int id)
        {
            var dicountCode = await _discountCodeService.GetByIdAsync(id);
            return Ok(dicountCode);
        }

        [Authorize(Roles = "Admin, Staff")]
        [HttpPost]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Create(CreateDiscountCodeDto dto)
        {
            var discountCode = await _discountCodeService.CreateAsync(dto);
            return CreatedAtAction(nameof(GetById), new { id = discountCode.Id }, discountCode);
        }

        [Authorize(Roles = "Admin, Staff")]
        [HttpPut("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Update(int id, UpdateDiscountCodeDto dto)
        {
            await _discountCodeService.UpdateAsync(id, dto);
            return NoContent();
        }

    }
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using ShopBackend.Application.DTOs;
using ShopBackend.Application.Interfaces;
using static System.Runtime.InteropServices.JavaScript.JSType;


namespace ShopBackend.API.Controllers
{

    [ApiController]
    [Route("api/[controller]")]

    public class InvoiceController : ControllerBase
    {
        private readonly IInvoiceService _invoiceService;

        public InvoiceController(IInvoiceService invoiceService)
        {
            _invoiceService = invoiceService;
        }


        [Authorize(Roles = "Admin")]
        [HttpGet]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetAll()
        {
            var invoices = await _invoiceService.GetAllAsync();
            return Ok(invoices);
        }


        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")]
        [HttpGet("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetById(int id)
        {
            var invoice = await _invoiceService.GetByIdAsync(id);
            return Ok(invoice);
        }


        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")]
        [HttpGet("byOrderId/{orderId}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetByOrderId(int orderId)
        {
            var invoice = await _invoiceService.GetByOrderIdAsync(orderId);
            return Ok(invoice); // <-- Das hier schickt JSON - Daten
        }


        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")]
        [HttpGet("byCustomerId/{customerId}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetByCustomerId(int customerId)
        {
            var invoices = await _invoiceService.GetByCustomerIdAsync(customerId);
            return Ok(invoices);
        }


        //[Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")]  Kunde muss Payment Method wählen, aber es gibt noch keine Invoice Id zur Orientierung --> Lösung über Handler verstehe ich nicht.
        [Authorize] // Ist Anfällig, Ein Kunde könnte Rechnungen für andere Kunden erstellen etc. --> Abfang im Service
        [HttpPost]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Create(CreateInvoiceDto dto)
        {
            var invoice = await _invoiceService.CreateAsync(dto);
            return CreatedAtAction(nameof(GetById), new { id = invoice.Id }, invoice);
        }


        [Authorize(Roles = "Admin, Staff")] // Policy wäre hier auch nice, ABER dann braucht es wieder neue DTOs und neue Methoden für Zahlungsstatus ändern etc. oder der Service
                                            // Müsste umgeschrieben werden, um böse Jungs abzufangen, die dann den Zahlungsstatus per Injection einfach auf bezahlt setzen wollen etc.
                                            // Ich muss leider ein paar business-logic Abstriche machen.
        [HttpPut("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Update(int id, UpdateInvoiceDto dto)
        {
            await _invoiceService.UpdateAsync(id, dto);
            return NoContent();
        }


    }
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using ShopBackend.Application.DTOs;
using ShopBackend.Application.Interfaces;
using System.Security.Principal;



namespace ShopBackend.API.Controllers
{
    [ApiController]
    [Route("api/[controller]")]
    
    public class OrderController : ControllerBase
    {
        private readonly IOrderService _orderService;

        public OrderController(IOrderService orderService)
        {
            _orderService = orderService;
        }


        [Authorize(Roles ="Admin")]
        [HttpGet]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetAll()
        {
            var orders = await _orderService.GetAllAsync();
            return Ok(orders);
        }

        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")] // neuer switch Handler kann das jetzt managen, theoretisch zumindest...
        [HttpGet("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetById(int id)
        {
            var order = await _orderService.GetByIdAsync(id);
            return Ok(order);
        }

        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")] // same
        [HttpGet("{orderId}/orderItems")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetOrderItemsByOrderId(int orderId)
        {
            var orderItems = await _orderService.GetOrderItemsByOrderIdAsync(orderId);
            return Ok(orderItems);
        }

        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")] // same
        [HttpGet("byCustomerId/{customerId}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetByCustomerId(int customerId)
        {
            var orders = await _orderService.GetByCustomerIdAsync(customerId);
            return Ok(orders);
        }

        [Authorize]
        [HttpPost]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Create(CreateOrderDto dto)
        {
            var order = await _orderService.CreateAsync(dto);
            return CreatedAtAction(nameof(GetById), new {id = order.Id}, order);
        }

        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")]
        [HttpPost("{orderId}/addOrderItem")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> AddOrderItem(int orderId, CreateOrderItemDto dto)
        {
            // nicht jeder Post muss ein 201 Created zurückgeben, hier wird zwar ein OrderItem im Service für die DB erstellt, aber es erfolgt kein direkter Rückgabewert, sondern sozusagen ein Put im Post-Pelz
            await _orderService.AddOrderItemAsync(orderId, dto);
            // deswegen NoContent() oder Ok() statt CreatedAtAction(...); 
            return NoContent();
        }

        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")]
        [HttpPut("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Update(int id, UpdateOrderDto dto)
        {
            await _orderService.UpdateAsync(id, dto);
            return NoContent();
        }

        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")]
        [HttpPut("{id}/cancel")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Cancel(int id)
        {
            await _orderService.CancelAsync(id);
            return NoContent();
        }

        [Authorize] // Multiple Ids kann mein Handler nicht handeln, daher bekommen die selbst mit dem Switchhandler nen Internen Security Check.
        // Die Ausgabe in der URL wäre hier z.B. bei order id=5 und orderItem id=3 :  api/order/5/orderItem/3
        [HttpPut("{orderId}/orderItem/{orderItemId}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> UpdateOrderItem(int orderId, int orderItemId, UpdateOrderItemDto dto)
        {
            await _orderService.UpdateOrderItemAsync(orderId, orderItemId, dto);
            return NoContent();
        }


        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")]
        [HttpDelete("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Delete(int id)
        {
            await _orderService.DeleteAsync(id);
            return NoContent();
        }


        [Authorize] // Multiple Ids kann mein Handler nicht handeln, daher bekommen die selbst mit dem Switchhandler nen Internen Security Check.
        [HttpDelete("{orderId}/orderItem/{orderItemId}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> RemoveOrderItem(int orderId, int orderItemId)
        {
            await _orderService.RemoveOrderItemAsync(orderId, orderItemId);
            return NoContent();
        }

    }
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using ShopBackend.Application.DTOs;
using ShopBackend.Application.Interfaces;


namespace ShopBackend.Api.Controllers
{
    [ApiController]
    // keine Umlaute bei den HTTP Routen die in Klammern stehen z.b. [HttpDelete("{id}/hard")] da diese in URLs sonst Prozentenkodiert ausgegeben werden. z.b. löschen -> l%C3%B6schen 
    [Route("api/[controller]")]
    
    public class ProductController : ControllerBase
    {

        private readonly IProductStockService _productStockService;

        public ProductController(IProductStockService productStockService)
        {
            _productStockService = productStockService;
        }


        [Authorize (Roles = "Admin")]
        [HttpGet]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetAll()
        {
            var products = await _productStockService.GetAllAsync();
            return Ok(products);

        }

        [AllowAnonymous]
        [HttpGet("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetById(int id)
        {
            var product = await _productStockService.GetByIdAsync(id);
            return Ok(product);
        }

        [AllowAnonymous]
        [HttpGet("active")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetAllActive()
        {
            var products = await _productStockService.GetAllActiveAsync();
            return Ok(products);
        }


        /*CreatedAtAction gibt HTTP 201 zurück und setzt einen Location Header in der Response:

            * nameof(GetById) -> der Name des Endpoints wo man das neue Produkt finden kann
            * new { id = product.Id } -> der Route-Parameter für diesen Endpoint z.b. id = 5 (api/product/5)
            * product -> das erstellte Objekt als Response Body

            Also die Response sagt praktisch: "Erstellt! Du findest es hier: api/product/5
        */
        [Authorize(Roles = "Admin, Staff")]
        [HttpPost]
        public async Task <IActionResult> Create(CreateProductDto dto)
        {
            var product = await _productStockService.CreateAsync(dto);
            return CreatedAtAction(nameof(GetById), new { id = product.Id }, product);
            
        }

        [Authorize(Roles = "Admin, Staff")]
        [HttpPut("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Update(int id, UpdateProductDto dto)
        {
            await _productStockService.UpdateAsync(id, dto);
            return NoContent();  // Http 204 Standard für erfolgreiche Updates
        }

        [AllowAnonymous]
        [HttpGet("{id}/stock")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetStockByProductId(int id)
        {
            var stock = await _productStockService.GetStockByProductIdAsync(id);
            return Ok(stock);
        }

        [Authorize(Roles = "Admin, Staff")]
        [HttpPut("{id}/stock")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> UpdateStock(int id, UpdateStockDto dto) // product.Id ist kein gültiger Parameter hier.
        {
            await _productStockService.UpdateStockAsync(id, dto);
            return NoContent();
        }

        [Authorize(Roles = "Admin, Staff")]
        [HttpDelete("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> SoftDelete(int id)
        {
            await _productStockService.SoftDeleteAsync(id);
            return NoContent();
        }

        [Authorize(Roles = "Admin")]
        [HttpDelete("{id}/hard")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> HardDelete(int id)
        {
            await _productStockService.HardDeleteAsync(id);
            return NoContent();

        }


    }
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using ShopBackend.Application.DTOs;
using ShopBackend.Application.Interfaces;


namespace ShopBackend.API.Controllers
{
    [ApiController]
    [Route("api/[controller]")]
    public class UserController : ControllerBase
    {
        private readonly IUserService _userService;
        public UserController(IUserService userService)
        {
            _userService = userService;
        }

        [Authorize(Roles = "Admin")]
        [HttpGet]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetAll() // Admins haben über den Handler IMMER Zugriff, GetAll() nur für Admins
        {
            var users = await _userService.GetAllAsync();
            return Ok(users);
        }

        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")]
        [HttpGet("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> GetById(int id)
        {
            var user = await _userService.GetByIdAsync(id);
            return Ok(user);
        }


        [AllowAnonymous] // Dominiert über Policy oder andere Authorizations, lässt alle durch.
        [HttpPost]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Create(CreateUserDto dto)
        {
            var user = await _userService.CreateAsync(dto);
            return CreatedAtAction(nameof(GetById), new { id = user.Id }, user);
        }

        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")]
        [HttpPut("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Update(int id, UpdateUserDto dto)
        {
            await _userService.UpdateAsync(id, dto);
            return NoContent();
        }

        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")]
        [HttpPut("{id}/changePw")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> ChangePassword(int id, ChangePasswordDto dto)
        {
            await _userService.ChangePasswordAsync(id, dto);
            return NoContent();
        }

        [Authorize(Policy = "IsResourceOwner")]
        [HttpDelete("{id}")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> Delete(int id)
        {
            await _userService.DeleteAsync(id);
            return NoContent(); 
        }

        [Authorize(Roles = "Admin")]
        [HttpPut("{id}/role")]
        public async Task<IActionResult> UpdateRole(int id, UpdateUserRoleDto dto)
        {
            await _userService.UpdateRoleAsync(id, dto);
            return NoContent();
        }

    }
}
=== C:\Users\vmadmin\source\repos\Fachspezi_in_C\ShopBackend.API\Middleware\ExceptionMiddleware.cs ===
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http;
using System;

namespace ShopBackend.API.Middleware
{


    // Statt der Middleware hätte ich auch wie ganz am Anfang kurz angedacht auch Exceptions User-Spezifisch über Response-DTOs ausgeben können,
    // Allerdings wäre das einfach viel zu viel geworden (und würde die Services NOCH weiter aufblähen),
    // Daher jetzt knackig über einen Global-Exception-Handler:

    public class ExceptionMiddleware
    {
        private readonly RequestDelegate _next;

        public ExceptionMiddleware(RequestDelegate next)
        { 
            _next = next;
        }

        public async Task InvokeAsync(HttpContext context)
        {
            try
            {
                await _next(context);
            }
            catch (KeyNotFoundException ex)
            {
                context.Response.StatusCode = 404;
                await context.Response.WriteAsJsonAsync(new { error = ex.Message });
            }
            catch (ArgumentException ex)
            {
                context.Response.StatusCode = 400;
                await context.Response.WriteAsJsonAsync(new {error = ex.Message});
            }
            catch (UnauthorizedAccessException ex)
            {
                context.Response.StatusCode = 401;
                await context.Response.WriteAsJsonAsync(new { error = ex.Message });
            }
            catch (InvalidOperationException ex)
            {
                context.Response.StatusCode = 400;
                await context.Response.WriteAsJsonAsync(new { error = ex.Message });
            }
            catch (Exception ex) 
            {
                context.Response.StatusCode = 500;
                await context.Response.WriteAsJsonAsync(new
                {
                    error = "Es ist ein wildes Relaxo aufgetreten.",
                    detail = ex.Message,
                    innerDetail = ex.InnerException?.Message
                });
            }
        }
    }
}

    <script>
        //JS Section:

        const API_URL = "/api";
        const token = sessionStorage.getItem("jwt");
        const role = sessionStorage.getItem("role");

        if (!token || (role !== "Admin" && role !== "Staff")) {
            window.location.href = "index.html";
        }



        function show(id) {
            document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(s => s.classList.remove('active'));
            document.getElementById(id).classList.add('active');
            document.querySelectorAll('nav li').forEach(li => li.classList.remove('active-nav'));
            const navEl = document.getElementById('nav-' + id);
            if (navEl) navEl.classList.add('active-nav');
        }


        // Sollte nen Timestamp Fehler abfangen, weil im Auditlog auf der Html invalid Date angezeigt wurde, obwohl das Backend im Swagger rund lÃ¤uft.
        function formatTimestamp(raw) {
            if (!raw) return 'â€“';
            const d = new Date(raw);
            if (isNaN(d.getTime()) || d.getFullYear() < 2000) return '(kein Datum)';
            return d.toLocaleString('de-DE');
        }

        // PRODUKTE & LAGER

        function resetProductForm() {
            document.getElementById('p-id').value = "";
            document.getElementById('p-name').value = "";
            document.getElementById('p-price').value = "";
            document.getElementById('btn-p-save').innerText = "âž• Erstellen";
            document.getElementById('btn-p-cancel').style.display = "none";
        }


        function editProduct(id, name, price, tax, isActive) {
            document.getElementById('p-id').value = id;
            document.getElementById('p-name').value = name;
            document.getElementById('p-price').value = price;
            document.getElementById('p-tax').value = tax;
            document.getElementById('p-active').value = isActive ? "true" : "false";
            document.getElementById('btn-p-save').innerText = "ðŸ’¾ Aktualisieren";
            document.getElementById('btn-p-cancel').style.display = "inline-block";
        }


        async function saveProduct() {
            const id = document.getElementById('p-id').value;
            const dto = {
                name: document.getElementById('p-name').value,
                price: parseFloat(document.getElementById('p-price').value),
                taxRate: parseFloat(document.getElementById('p-tax').value),
                isActive: document.getElementById('p-active').value === "true"
            };
            const url = id ? `${API_URL}/product/${id}` : `${API_URL}/product`;
            const method = id ? 'PUT' : 'POST';
            const res = await fetch(url, {
                method,
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` },
                body: JSON.stringify(dto)
            });
            if (res.ok) { resetProductForm(); loadProducts(); }
            else alert("Fehler beim Speichern des Produkts.");
        }



        async function loadProducts() {
            const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/product`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } });
            const products = await res.json();
            const tbody = document.querySelector("#table-products tbody");

            let statTotalItems = 0, statReservedItems = 0, statInventoryValue = 0;

            tbody.innerHTML = products.map(p => {
                const isDeleted = p.isDeleted;
                const stockQty = p.stock ? p.stock.quantity : 0;
                const resQty = p.stock ? p.stock.reservedQuantity : 0;
                const available = stockQty - resQty;

                const statusBadge = isDeleted
                    ? `<span class="badge badge-inactive">Verborgen</span>`
                    : (p.isActive ? `<span class="badge badge-active">Aktiv</span>` : `<span class="badge badge-inactive">Inaktiv</span>`);

                if (!isDeleted) {
                    statTotalItems += stockQty;
                    statReservedItems += resQty;
                    statInventoryValue += (stockQty * p.price);
                }

                const softDeleteBtn = isDeleted
                    ? `<button class="btn-small" style="background:#27ae60;color:white;" onclick="toggleSoftDelete(${p.id}, false)" title="Reaktivieren">Anzeigen</button>`
                    : `<button class="btn-small" style="background:#e67e22;color:white;" onclick="toggleSoftDelete(${p.id}, true)"  title="Verbergen">Verbergen</button>`;

                return `
                        <tr style="${isDeleted ? 'background:#fff5f5;' : ''}">
                            <td>${p.id}</td>
                            <td><strong>${p.name}</strong><br>${statusBadge}</td>
                            <td>
                                <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:5px;">
                                    <input type="number" id="st-qty-${p.id}" value="${stockQty}" style="width:60px;padding:4px;">
                                    <button class="btn-small btn-success" onclick="updateStock(${p.id})">ðŸ’¾</button>
                                </div>
                            </td>
                            <td style="color:#f39c12;font-weight:bold;">ðŸ”’ ${resQty}</td>
                            <td style="font-weight:bold;">${available}</td>
                            <td>${p.price.toFixed(2)}â‚¬</td>
                            <td>
                                <div style="display:flex;gap:5px;">
                                    <button class="btn-small btn-warning" onclick="editProduct(${p.id}, '${p.name.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}', ${p.price}, ${p.taxRate}, ${p.isActive})">Edit</button>
                                    ${softDeleteBtn}
                                    ${role === 'Admin' ? `<button class="btn-small btn-danger" onclick="hardDeleteProduct(${p.id})">LÃ¶schen</button>` : ''}
                                </div>
                            </td>
                        </tr>`;
            }).join("");

            document.getElementById('stat-total-items').innerText = statTotalItems;
            document.getElementById('stat-reserved-items').innerText = statReservedItems;
            document.getElementById('stat-inventory-value').innerText = statInventoryValue.toFixed(2) + " â‚¬";
        }



        async function updateStock(productId) {
            const getRes = await fetch(`${API_URL}/product/${productId}/stock`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } });
            const stock = await getRes.json();
            const newQty = parseInt(document.getElementById(`st-qty-${productId}`).value);

            if (isNaN(newQty) || newQty < 0)
            {
                alert("UngÃ¼ltige Menge!");
                return;
            }
            const dto = { quantity: newQty, reservedQuantity: stock.reservedQuantity };
            const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/product/${productId}/stock`, {
                method: 'PUT',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` },
                body: JSON.stringify(dto)
            });
            if (res.ok) loadProducts();
            else { alert("Fehler beim Lagerupdate:\n" + await res.text()); loadProducts(); }
        }



        async function toggleSoftDelete(id, shouldDelete) {
            if (!confirm(`Produkt wirklich ${shouldDelete ? 'verbergen' : 'wieder anzeigen'}?`)) return;
            const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/product/${id}`, {
                method: 'DELETE',
                headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` }
            });
            if (res.ok) loadProducts();
            else alert("Fehler beim Ã„ndern des Sichtbarkeitsstatus.");
        }



        async function hardDeleteProduct(id) {
            if (!confirm("ACHTUNG: Produkt endgÃ¼ltig aus Datenbank lÃ¶schen? (Geht nur wenn Lager = 0)")) return;
            const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/product/${id}/hard`, { method: 'DELETE', headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } });
            if (res.ok) loadProducts();
            else alert("Fehler: Produkt hat evtl. noch Lagerbestand.");
        }


        // RABATTCODES

        async function loadDiscounts() {
            const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/discountcode`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } });
            const data = await res.json();
            document.querySelector("#table-discounts tbody").innerHTML = data.map(d => `
                    <tr>
                        <td>${d.id}</td>
                        <td><strong>${d.code}</strong></td>
                        <td>${d.discountPercentage}%</td>
                        <td>${d.minOrderValue.toFixed(2)}â‚¬</td>
                        <td>${d.usedCount} / ${d.maxUses}</td>
                        <td><button class="btn-small btn-warning" onclick="openDiscountModal(${d.id})">âœï¸ Bearbeiten</button></td>
                    </tr>`).join("");
        }

        async function createDiscount() {
            const codeVal = document.getElementById('d-code').value;
            const percVal = parseFloat(document.getElementById('d-perc').value);
            const minVal = parseFloat(document.getElementById('d-min').value);
            const usesVal = parseInt(document.getElementById('d-uses').value);
            const startVal = document.getElementById('d-start').value;
            const endVal = document.getElementById('d-end').value;

            if (!codeVal || isNaN(percVal)) {
                return alert("Code und Prozentsatz sind Pflichtfelder!");
            }

            const dto = {
                code: codeVal,
                discountPercentage: percVal,
                minOrderValue: isNaN(minVal) ? 0 : minVal, // Hotfix fÃ¼r NaN || 0 -> 0, ist zwar okay aber nicht Konsistent.
                maxUses: isNaN(usesVal) ? 100 : usesVal,
                validFrom: startVal || null, 
                validTo: endVal || null      
            };

            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/discountcode`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                        'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}`
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify(dto)
                });

                if (res.ok) {
                    // Formular leeren
                    document.getElementById('d-code').value = "";
                    document.getElementById('d-perc').value = "";
                    document.getElementById('d-min').value = "";
                    document.getElementById('d-start').value = "";
                    document.getElementById('d-end').value = "";
                    loadDiscounts();
                } else {
                    const errorMsg = await res.text();
                    alert("Fehler beim Anlegen: " + errorMsg);
                }
            } catch (err) {
                console.error("Netzwerkfehler:", err);
            }
        }

        async function openDiscountModal(id)
        {
            const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/discountcode/${id}`, {
                headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` }
            });
            if (!res.ok) return alert("Fehler beim Laden des Codes");
            const d = await res.json();

            document.getElementById('modal-d-id').value = d.id;
            document.getElementById('modal-d-code').value = d.code;
            document.getElementById('modal-d-perc').value = d.discountPercentage;
            document.getElementById('modal-d-min').value = d.minOrderValue;
            document.getElementById('modal-d-uses').value = d.maxUses;

            // Daten fÃ¼r datetime-local formatieren (YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM)
            if (d.validFrom) document.getElementById('modal-d-start').value = d.validFrom.substring(0, 16);
            if (d.validTo) document.getElementById('modal-d-end').value = d.validTo.substring(0, 16);

            document.getElementById('discount-modal').classList.add('open');
        }

        function closeDiscountModal()
        {
            document.getElementById('discount-modal').classList.remove('open');
        }


        async function saveDiscountEdit() {
            const id = document.getElementById('modal-d-id').value;
            const dto = {
                code: document.getElementById('modal-d-code').value,
                discountPercentage: parseFloat(document.getElementById('modal-d-perc').value),
                minOrderValue: parseFloat(document.getElementById('modal-d-min').value),
                maxUses: parseInt(document.getElementById('modal-d-uses').value),
                validFrom: document.getElementById('modal-d-start').value || null, 
                validTo: document.getElementById('modal-d-end').value || null      // falsche Variablennamen... wer das nur wieder war -.-
            };

            const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/discountcode/${id}`, {
                method: 'PUT',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}`
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(dto)
            });

            if (res.ok) {
                closeDiscountModal();
                loadDiscounts();
            } else {
                const txt = await res.text();
                alert("Fehler beim Speichern: " + txt);
            }
        }


        // BESTELLUNGEN

        // FÃ¼r mein ZukÃ¼nftiges Ich:
        // Kritische Funktion 
        // Wenn mal wieder irgendwas bei den Bestellungen nicht im Frontend angezeigt wird, ist der Fehler mit hoher Wahrscheinlichkeit hier im LoadOrders bzw.SaveOrder()
        async function loadOrders() {
            const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/order`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } });
            const orders = await res.json();
            document.querySelector("#table-orders tbody").innerHTML = orders.map(o => `
                    <tr>
                        <td>${o.id}</td>
                        <td>Kunde #${o.customerId}</td>
                        <td>${formatTimestamp(o.orderDate)}</td>
                        <td><strong>${o.status}</strong></td>
                        <td>${o.grossTotal.toFixed(2)}â‚¬</td>
                        <td style="display:flex;gap:4px;flex-wrap:wrap;">
                            <button class="btn-small btn-accent"   onclick="openOrderModal(${o.id})">âœï¸ Bearbeiten</button>
                            ${o.status !== 'storniert' ? `<button class="btn-small btn-warning" onclick="cancelOrderAdmin(${o.id})">Stornieren</button>` : ''}
                            ${role === 'Admin' ? `<button class="btn-small btn-danger" onclick="deleteOrderAdmin(${o.id})">LÃ¶schen</button>` : ''}
                        </td>
                    </tr>`).join("");
        }

        async function cancelOrderAdmin(id) {
            if (!confirm("Bestellung wirklich stornieren?")) return;
            await fetch(`${API_URL}/order/${id}/cancel`, { method: 'PUT', headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } });
            loadOrders();
        }

        async function deleteOrderAdmin(id) {
            if (!confirm("Order komplett aus DB lÃ¶schen?")) return;
            await fetch(`${API_URL}/order/${id}`, { method: 'DELETE', headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } });
            loadOrders();
        }

        // MODAL
        let _modalOrderId = null;
        let _modalOrderItems = [];

        async function openOrderModal(orderId)
        {
            _modalOrderId = orderId;
            _modalOrderItems = [];

            document.getElementById('modal-order-id-title').textContent = `#${orderId}`;
            document.getElementById('modal-items-list').innerHTML = '<p style="padding:12px;color:#888;">Ladeâ€¦</p>';
            document.getElementById('modal-discount').value = '';
            document.getElementById('order-modal').classList.add('open');

            const orderRes = await fetch(`${API_URL}/order/${orderId}`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } });
            if (!orderRes.ok)
            {
                alert("Bestellung konnte nicht geladen werden.");
                return;
            }
            const order = await orderRes.json();

            if (order.status)
            {
                document.getElementById('modal-status').value = order.status;
            }

            if (order.discountCode)
            {
                document.getElementById('modal-discount').value = order.discountCode;
            }

            const itemsRes = await fetch(`${API_URL}/order/${orderId}/orderItems`,
                {
                    headers:
                    {
                        'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}`
                    }
                });
            if (!itemsRes.ok)
            {
                document.getElementById('modal-items-list').innerHTML = '<p style="padding:12px;color:var(--danger)">Positionen konnten nicht geladen werden.</p>';
                return;
            }

            const items = await itemsRes.json();
            _modalOrderItems = items;

            if (!items || items.length === 0) {
                document.getElementById('modal-items-list').innerHTML = '<p style="padding:12px;color:#aaa;">Keine Positionen vorhanden.</p>';
                return;
            }

            document.getElementById('modal-items-list').innerHTML = items.map(item => `
              <div class="order-item-row" id="row-item-${item.id}">
                <span><strong>${item.product?.name ?? 'GelÃ¶schtes Produkt #' + item.productId}</strong></span>
                <input type="number" id="item-qty-${item.id}" value="${item.quantity}" min="0">
                <button class="btn-small btn-danger" onclick="removeItemRow(${item.id})">ðŸ—‘ï¸</button>
              </div>`)
             .join("");
        }


        function closeOrderModal() {
            document.getElementById('order-modal').classList.remove('open');
            _modalOrderId = null;
            _modalOrderItems = [];
        }


        async function cancelOrderFromModal() {
            if (!_modalOrderId) return;
            if (!confirm(`Bestellung #${_modalOrderId} wirklich stornieren?`)) return;
            await cancelOrderAdmin(_modalOrderId);
            closeOrderModal();
        }


        function removeItemRow(itemId)
        {
            const input = document.getElementById(`item-qty-${itemId}`);
            const row = document.getElementById(`row-item-${itemId}`);

            if (input && row)
            {
                input.value = 0;
                input.disabled = true; // super wichtig 
                row.style.opacity = "0.3";
                row.style.background = "#fee";
            }
        }

     
        // Kritische Funktion
        async function saveOrder() {
            if (!_modalOrderId) return;

            const orderItems = _modalOrderItems.map(item => {
                const input = document.getElementById(`item-qty-${item.id}`);
                // parseInt liefert NaN, wenn das Feld leer ist oder Text enthÃ¤lt
                let qty = input ? parseInt(input.value) : item.quantity;

                // Sicherheitsnetz: Wenn NaN oder negativ, wirds auf 0 gesetzt (=lÃ¶schen)
                if (isNaN(qty) || qty < 0) {
                    qty = 0;
                }

                return {
                    orderItemId: item.id,
                    quantity: qty
                };
            });

            // Restliche Daten
            const discountCode = document.getElementById('modal-discount').value.trim();
            const statusVal = document.getElementById('modal-status').value;

            const dto = {
                status: statusVal || null,
                discountCode: discountCode || null,
                orderItems: orderItems
            };

            // Request abschicken
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/order/${_modalOrderId}`, {
                    method: 'PUT',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                        'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}`
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify(dto)
                });

                if (res.ok) {
                    closeOrderModal();
                    loadOrders();
                } else {
                    const errorText = await res.text();
                    alert("Fehler beim Speichern:\n" + (errorText || res.status));
                }
            } catch (err) {
                console.error("Netzwerkfehler:", err);
                alert("Verbindung zum Server fehlgeschlagen.");
            }
        }





        // RECHNUNGEN

        async function loadInvoices() {
            const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/invoice`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } });
            const data = await res.json();
            document.querySelector("#table-invoices tbody").innerHTML = data.map(i => `
                    <tr>
                        <td>${i.id}</td>
                        <td>Order #${i.orderId}</td>
                        <td>${i.firstName} ${i.lastName}</td>
                        <td><span class="badge ${i.status === 'bezahlt' ? 'badge-active' : 'badge-inactive'}">${i.status}</span></td>
                        <td>${i.paymentMethod}</td>
                        <td>${i.grossTotal.toFixed(2)}â‚¬</td>
                        <td>
                        <button class="btn-small btn-warning" onclick="updateInvoice(${i.id}, '${i.status}', '${i.paymentMethod}')">âœï¸ Bearbeiten</button>
                        <button class="btn-small btn-accent" onclick="downloadInvoiceJSON(${i.id})"> Rechnung laden </button> 
                        </td>
                    </tr>`).join("");
        }



        async function updateInvoice(id, currentStatus, currentMethod) {
            // Status abfragen (wie bisher)
            const newStatus = prompt("Neuer Status (bezahlt, offen, storniert):", currentStatus);
            if (newStatus === null) return; // Wenn du auf Abbrechen klickst

            // Zahlungsart abfragen (NEU)
            const newMethod = prompt("Neue Zahlungsart (Barzahlung, ELV, PayPal, Rechnung):", currentMethod);
            if (newMethod === null) return; // Wenn du auf Abbrechen klickst

            // Beides ans Backend schicken
            await fetch(`${API_URL}/invoice/${id}`, {
                method: 'PUT',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    status: newStatus,
                    paymentMethod: newMethod // <--- Die Bezahlart wird jetzt mitgeschickt!
                })
            });

            // Neu: PrÃ¼fung ob der PUT erfolgreich war, ansonsten Fehlerausgabe. 
            if (!res.ok)
            {
                alert("Fehler: " + await res.text()); return;
            }

            loadInvoices();
        }



        async function downloadInvoiceJSON(invoiceId)
        {
            try
            {
                // Holt die Rechnung vom Backend 
                const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/invoice/${invoiceId}`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } });
                if (!res.ok) throw new Error("Rechnung konnte nicht geladen werden.");
                const data = await res.json();

                let positionen = [];
                let steuerAufschluesselung = {};

                // Positionen durchgehen und mappen
                if (data.order && data.order.orderItems)
                {
                    positionen = data.order.orderItems.map(item =>
                    {
                        const steuerSatz = item.taxRate || 19; // Fallback, falls mal was leer ist

                        // Steuern aufsummieren fÃ¼r die Ãœbersicht am Ende (z.B. "19%": 5.40, "7%": 1.20)
                        if (!steuerAufschluesselung[`${steuerSatz}%`]) steuerAufschluesselung[`${steuerSatz}%`] = 0;
                        steuerAufschluesselung[`${steuerSatz}%`] += item.taxAmount;

                        return {                        
                            Produkt: item.product ? item.product.name : "GelÃ¶schtes Produkt",
                            Menge: item.quantity,
                            EinzelpreisNetto: item.unitPrice.toFixed(2) + " â‚¬",
                            Steuersatz: steuerSatz + "%",
                            SteuerBetrag: item.taxAmount.toFixed(2) + " â‚¬",
                            ZeilenSummeBrutto: (item.lineTotal + item.taxAmount).toFixed(2) + " â‚¬"
                        };
                    });
                }

                // Auf Rabattcode prÃ¼fen
                let rabattInfo = null;
                if (data.order && data.order.discountCode) {
                    rabattInfo = `${data.order.discountCode.code} (${data.order.discountCode.discountPercentage}% Rabatt)`;
                }

                // Neues JSON Objekt zusammenbauen
                const cleanInvoice =
                {
                    RechnungsNummer: data.id,
                    BestellNummer: data.orderId,
                    RechnungsDatum: data.paidAt ? new Date(data.paidAt).toLocaleString() : "Ausstehend",
                    Kunde: `${data.firstName} ${data.lastName}`,
                    Adresse: data.address,
                    Zahlungsart: data.paymentMethod,
                    Status: data.status,
                    Rabatt: rabattInfo || "Kein Rabatt angewendet",
                    Positionen: positionen,
                    SteuerAufschluesselung: steuerAufschluesselung, // Zeigt hier z.B. 19% und 7% separat an
                    Gesamtbetraege: {
                        NettoGesamt: data.netTotal.toFixed(2) + " â‚¬",
                        SteuerGesamt: data.taxAmount.toFixed(2) + " â‚¬",
                        "BruttoGesamt (Inkl. Rabatt)": data.grossTotal.toFixed(2) + " â‚¬"
                    }
                };

                // Dateigenerierung und Download-Trigger
                const jsonString = JSON.stringify(cleanInvoice, null, 2);
                const blob = new Blob([jsonString], { type: "application/json" });
                const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
                const a = document.createElement('a');
                a.href = url;
                a.download = `Rechnung_${cleanInvoice.RechnungsNummer}_Bestellung_${cleanInvoice.BestellNummer}.json`;
                document.body.appendChild(a);
                a.click();
                document.body.removeChild(a);
                URL.revokeObjectURL(url);

            }
            catch (err)
            {
                alert("Fehler beim JSON-Download: " + err.message);
            }
        }

        async function loadCustomers() {

                const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/customer`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } });

                            <td>${c.firstName} ${c.lastName}</td>
                            <td>${c.address}<br><small>ðŸ“ž ${c.phone || 'Keine Nummer'}</small></td>
                            <td>
                                <div style="display:flex;gap:5px;">
                                    <button class="btn-small btn-warning"
                                            onclick="editCustomer(${c.id}, '${c.firstName.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}', '${c.lastName.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}', '${c.address.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}', '${(c.phone || '').replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">
                                        Bearbeiten
                                    </button>
                                    ${role === 'Admin' ? `<button class="btn-small btn-danger" onclick="deleteCustomer(${c.id})">LÃ¶schen</button>` : ''}
                                </div>
                            </td>
                        </tr>`).join("");
            } catch (err) { console.error("Fehler beim Laden der Kunden:", err); }
        }


        async function createCustomer() {
            const userIdVal = document.getElementById('c-userid').value;
            if (!userIdVal) return alert("User-ID fehlt!");
            const dto = {
                firstName: document.getElementById('c-firstname').value,
                lastName: document.getElementById('c-lastname').value,
                address: document.getElementById('c-address').value,
                phone: ""
            };
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/customer/${userIdVal}`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` },
                    body: JSON.stringify(dto)
                });
                if (res.ok) { alert("Kunde angelegt!"); loadCustomers(); }
                else alert(`Fehler ${res.status}: ` + await res.text());
            } catch (err) { console.error(err); }
        }

        async function editCustomer(id, fName, lName, addr, phone) {
            const newFirstName = prompt("Neuer Vorname:", fName); if (newFirstName === null) return;
            const newLastName = prompt("Neuer Nachname:", lName); if (newLastName === null) return;
            const newAddress = prompt("Neue Adresse:", addr); if (newAddress === null) return;
            const newPhone = prompt("Neue Telefonnummer:", phone); if (newPhone === null) return;
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/customer/${id}`, {
                    method: 'PUT',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ firstName: newFirstName, lastName: newLastName, address: newAddress, phone: newPhone })
                });
                if (res.ok) loadCustomers();
                else alert("Fehler beim Speichern: " + await res.text());
            } catch (err) { console.error(err); }
        }


        async function deleteCustomer(id) {
            if (!confirm("Kundenprofil wirklich lÃ¶schen?")) return;
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/customer/${id}`, { method: 'DELETE', headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } });
                if (!res.ok) alert(await res.text());
                loadCustomers();
            } catch (err) { console.error(err); }
        }




        // USER & ROLLEN

        async function createUser() {
            const dto = {
                email: document.getElementById('u-email').value,
                password: document.getElementById('u-password').value,
                role: parseInt(document.getElementById('u-role').value)
            };
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/user`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` },
                    body: JSON.stringify(dto)
                });
                if (res.ok) {
                    document.getElementById('u-email').value = "";
                    document.getElementById('u-password').value = "";
                    loadUsers();
                } else alert("Fehler beim User anlegen:\n" + await res.text());
            } catch (err) { console.error(err); }
        }


        async function loadUsers() {
            const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/user`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } });
            const users = await res.json();
            document.querySelector("#table-users tbody").innerHTML = users.map(u => `
                    <tr>
                        <td>${u.id}</td>
                        <td>${u.email}</td>
                        <td style="font-weight:bold;color:#2c3e50;">${u.role}</td>
                        <td>
                            <div style="display:flex;gap:10px;align-items:center;">
                                <select id="role-select-${u.id}" style="padding:5px;border-radius:4px;">
                                    <option value="" disabled selected>Rolle Ã¤ndernâ€¦</option>
                                    <option value="0">Admin</option>
                                    <option value="20">Staff</option>
                                    <option value="50">Customer</option>
                                    <option value="99">Inaktiv</option>
                                </select>
                                <button class="btn-success" style="padding:5px 10px;width:auto;" onclick="updateRoleFromSelect(${u.id})">Speichern</button>
                                ${u.id !== 1 ? `<button class="btn-danger" style="padding:5px 10px;width:auto;margin-left:10px;" onclick="deleteUser(${u.id})">ðŸ—‘ï¸</button>` : '<span style="margin-left:10px;">ðŸ”’</span>'}
                            </div>
                        </td>
                    </tr>`).join("");
        }


        async function updateRoleFromSelect(id) {
            const selectElement = document.getElementById(`role-select-${id}`);
            const newRole = parseInt(selectElement.value);

            // Neu: Auf isNaN prÃ¼fen, nicht auf !newRole, vorher konnte kein Admin gesetzt werden als Rolle, alles andere ging aber.
            if (isNaN(newRole)) {
                alert("Bitte erst eine neue Rolle auswÃ¤hlen!");
                return;
            }

            if (!confirm(`User #${id} wirklich auf die Rolle "${selectElement.options[selectElement.selectedIndex].text}" setzen?`)) return;

            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/user/${id}/role`, {
                    method: 'PUT',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ role: newRole })
                });
                if (res.ok) { alert("Rolle geÃ¤ndert!"); loadUsers(); }
                else alert("Fehler: " + await res.text());
            } catch (err) { console.error(err); }
        }


        async function deleteUser(id) {
            if (!confirm("User komplett aus dem System lÃ¶schen?")) return;
            const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/user/${id}`, { method: 'DELETE', headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } });
            if (!res.ok) alert(await res.text());
            loadUsers();
        }




        // AUDIT LOGS

        async function loadLogs() {
            const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/auditlog`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } });
            const logs = await res.json();
            logs.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.changedAt) - new Date(a.changedAt));
            document.querySelector("#table-logs tbody").innerHTML = logs.map(l => `
                    <tr>
                        <td>${formatTimestamp(l.changedAt)}</td> 
                        <td><strong>${l.changedBy}</strong></td>
                        <td><span class="badge badge-active">${l.action}</span></td>
                        <td>${l.entityName} #${l.entityId}</td>
                        <td style="font-size:0.85em;color:#555;">${l.details}</td>
                    </tr>`).join("");
        }

            sessionStorage.clear();
            window.location.href = "index.html";

    // Neue Index-Seite, ohne jegliche Infos, einfach nur Login.
        const API_URL = "/api";

        async function login() {
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`${API_URL}/auth/login`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({
                        email: document.getElementById('email').value,
                        password: document.getElementById('password').value
                    })
                });

                const data = await response.json();
                if (!response.ok) throw new Error(data.error || "Login fehlgeschlagen");

                // Alles in den SessionStorage
                sessionStorage.setItem("jwt", data.token);
                sessionStorage.setItem("userId", data.id);
                sessionStorage.setItem("role", data.role);
                sessionStorage.setItem("customerId", data.customerId); // Kommt direkt vom DTO

                const userRole = String(data.role);

                // Weiterleitung
                if (userRole === "Admin" || userRole === "0")
                {
                    window.location.href = "Admin.html";
                }
                else if (userRole === "Staff" || userRole === "20")
                {
                    window.location.href = "Staff.html";
                }
                else
                {
                    window.location.href = "Shop.html";
                }

            }
            catch (err)
            {
                alert(err.message);
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>
